SELECT n."Id", n."Channel", n."Content", n."CreatedAt", n."Error", n."RetryCount", n."SentAt", n."Status", n."Type", n."UserId"
FROM notifications AS n
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT u."Id", u."IsDeleted"
    FROM users AS u
    WHERE NOT (u."IsDeleted")
) AS u0 ON n."UserId" = u0."Id"
WHERE NOT (u0."IsDeleted") AND n."Status" = 'Pending' AND n."RetryCount" < 3
ORDER BY n."CreatedAt"
LIMIT @__p_0
